GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_t*sin(log(A + c3))

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT:** `-0.4537*A*exp(-0.08462*t) + 0.7535*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has two terms:
1. `A*exp(-c*t)` ŌĆö an exponential decay in t multiplied by A
2. `sin(log(A + 1))` ŌĆö a sine of logarithm function

The key challenge is that `sin(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function. None of the candidates contain `sin(...)` explicitly. So I need to check whether any combination of the basis functions in the candidates can exactly reproduce `sin(log(A+1))`.

Let me examine the basis functions available in the candidates:
- `A` (linear)
- `A*exp(c*t)` (exponential in t times A)
- `1/(A+c)` or `A/(A+c)` (rational functions of A)
- `exp(A*c)` (exponential in A)
- `log(A*c + 1)` (logarithm)
- `A**c` (power law)
- `Max(0, A)` (ReLU)
- `Abs(A)**c` (absolute power)
- `tanh(...)` (hyperbolic tangent)
- `A/sqrt(c+t)` (inverse square root)

**Critical observation:** `sin(log(A+1))` cannot be expressed as any finite linear combination of:
- polynomials in A
- `exp(c*A)`
- `log(A+1)`
- rational functions of A
- `A^c` (power functions)

These are all linearly independent basis functions, and `sin(log(A+1))` is not in the span of any of them. The function `sin(log(A+1))` oscillates (albeit slowly for large A), while none of the candidate basis functions oscillate in A.

For candidates with `A*exp(c*t)`: this can match the first GT term by setting the constant appropriately.

But the second term `sin(log(A+1))` requires a `sin` function, which NO candidate provides. No combination of `log`, `exp`, polynomials, rational functions, or power functions can produce `sin(log(A+1))`.

Let me verify: Could `sin(log(A+1))` be zero? No, c2*_t = 0.7535, which is nonzero.

Could we set c2=0 in the GT? No ŌĆö GT constants are FIXED.

Therefore, **no candidate can match the GT**, because none contain a `sin` (or equivalent oscillatory) basis function.

Let me do a quick check on all candidates to confirm none have `sin`:
- Candidates 1-50: I see `exp`, `log`, `Max`, `Abs`, `tanh`, `sqrt`, polynomial terms, but NO `sin` or `cos` anywhere.

Since `sin(log(A+1))` with coefficient 0.7535 is a required, non-zero component of the GT, and it cannot be represented by any combination of the basis functions available in any candidate, none can match.
